### Chemistry

- `L.11`
  Equation:

  \[x_{\mathrm{L_11}}^{+,\mathrm{chem}} = K_{\mathrm{L_11}} x_{\mathrm{L_11}}^{-,\mathrm{chem}}, \qquad \mathbf{1}^T K_{\mathrm{L_11}} = \mathbf{1}^T\]

  Variable legend: `x=[m_source,m_volatile,m_liquid,m_essence,m_fixed]^T`; `K_line` conserves total material.
  Reading: opaque operator line.
  Confidence: strong

- `L.14`
  Equation:

  \[x_{\mathrm{L_14}}^{+,\mathrm{chem}} = K_{\mathrm{L_14}} x_{\mathrm{L_14}}^{-,\mathrm{chem}}, \qquad \mathbf{1}^T K_{\mathrm{L_14}} = \mathbf{1}^T\]

- `L.11`

  Variable legend: `X^(phys)` tracks containment geometry, phase, pressure, and seal integrity.
  Reading: opaque operator line.
  Confidence: strong

## Direct Operational Meaning

A control-theory page: it formalizes the stability doctrine in paragraph form — repetition plus clamps yields convergence (purity as fixed-point). Process statistics: 105 circulation commands (qo-); 24 valve/clamp checkpoints (ckh/kch); 35 infusion-stabilize cycles (shedy); 4 completion markers (daiin); 3 salt/crystallization references (sal).

## Mathematical Extraction

Across the formal lenses, `f76r` behaves as a fixed-point purification page with N_qo=61, N_valve=7, and N_seal=2. The governing update is x_(n+1) = V(C(x_n)); stop when ||x_(n+1)-x_n|| <= eps, then publish y = S(x_*).

## Mythic Extraction

`f76r` is a bathhouse-laboratory chamber: descend through linked pools, purify by circulation, prove stability at the clamps, and only then carry the living fluid onward.

## All-Lens Zero Point

`A control-theory page: it formalizes the stability doctrine in paragraph form — repetition plus clamps yields convergence (purity as fixed-point).`

## Formal Mathematical Overlay For F76R

### Imported Kernel Equations

\[\mathcal H := L^2(\widehat{\mathbb C}, \mu), \qquad \rho \in \mathcal T_1(\mathcal H), \qquad \rho \succeq 0, \qquad \mathrm{Tr}(\rho)=1\]

\[\mathcal H_{\mathrm{tot}} = \left(\bigoplus_r \mathcal H_r\right) \oplus \left(\bigoplus_e \mathcal H_{\Lambda_e}\right) \oplus \mathcal H_{\mathrm{fail}}\]

\[x_{n+1}^{\mathrm{chem}} = K_n x_n^{\mathrm{chem}}, \qquad \mathbf{1}^T K_n = \mathbf{1}^T\]

\[g = \mathrm{Coll}(X), \qquad X = \mathrm{Expand}(g) \oplus r\]

\[\Phi_j^{(\lambda)} = T_\lambda^{-1} \circ \Phi_j^{(\mathrm{AQM})} \circ T_\lambda\]

### Typed State Machine

\[
\mathcal R_{f76r} = \{r_{charge}, r_{circulate}, r_{clamp}, r_{commit}, r_{seal}\}
\]
\[
\delta(r_{charge})=r_{circulate}, \qquad
\delta(r_{circulate})=r_{clamp}, \qquad
\delta(r_{clamp})=
\begin{cases}
r_{circulate} & \text{if } \Delta_n > 0 \\
r_{commit} & \text{if } \Delta_n = 0
\end{cases}
\]
\[
\delta(r_{commit})=
\begin{cases}
r_{seal} & \text{if } P_{salt} = 1 \\
r_{circulate} & \text{otherwise}
\end{cases}
\]
